(**********************************************************************

 The enriched category of dialgebras

 We construct an enrichment over the category of dialgebras between
 two enriched functors. In addition, we show that this gives rise to
 inserters in the bicategory of enriched categories.

 Note that to construct this enrichment, we assume that the monoidal
 category `V` has equalizers. This is because morphisms in the
 category of dialgebras come with a requirement that a certain diagram
 commutes. As such, this requirement must also be present in the
 enrichment. To formulate this requirement, we use equalizers.

 Contents
 1. The enrichment of dialgebras
 2. Enrichment of the first projection
 3. Enrichment of functors to dialgebras
 4. Enrichment of natural transformations to dialgebras

 **********************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Isos.

Require Import UniMath.CategoryTheory.Core.Functors.

Local Open Scope cat.
Local Open Scope moncat.

Section EnrichedDialgebras.
  Context (V : monoidal_cat)
          (EV : Equalizers V)
          {C₁ C₂ : category}
          {F G : C₁ ⟶ C₂}
          {E₁ : enrichment C₁ V}
          {E₂ : enrichment C₂ V}
          (FE : functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂)
          (GE : functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂).

  (**
   1. The enrichment of dialgebras
   *)
  Definition dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left
             {x y : C₁}
             (f : F x --> G x)
             (g : F y --> G y)
    : E₁ ⦃ x , y ⦄ --> E₂ ⦃ F x , G y ⦄
    := GE x y · precomp_arr _ _ f.

  Definition dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right
             {x y : C₁}
             (f : F x --> G x)
             (g : F y --> G y)
    : E₁ ⦃ x , y ⦄ --> E₂ ⦃ F x , G y ⦄
    := FE x y · postcomp_arr _ _ g.

  Definition dialgebra_enrichment_mor
             {x y : C₁}
             (f : F x --> G x)
             (g : F y --> G y)
    : V
    := EV _ _
         (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f g)
         (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f g).

  Definition dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl
             {x y : C₁}
             (f : F x --> G x)
             (g : F y --> G y)
    : dialgebra_enrichment_mor f g --> E₁ ⦃ x , y ⦄
    := EqualizerArrow
         (EV _ _
             (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f g)
             (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f g)).

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f g =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f g

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f g =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f g

    exact (EqualizerEqAr
             (EV _ _
                (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f g)
                (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f g))).
  Qed.

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
v: V
φ₁, φ₂: V ⟦ v, dialgebra_enrichment_mor f g ⟧
p: φ₁ · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g =
φ₂ · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g
φ₁ = φ₂

V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
v: V
φ₁, φ₂: V ⟦ v, dialgebra_enrichment_mor f g ⟧
p: φ₁ · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g =
φ₂ · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g
φ₁
· pr21 (EV (E₁ ⦃ x, y ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x, G y ⦄)
          (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f g)
          (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f g)) =
φ₂
· pr21 (EV (E₁ ⦃ x, y ⦄) (E₂ ⦃ F x, G y ⦄)
          (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f g)
          (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f g))

    exact p.
  Qed.

f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
enriched_id E₁ x · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f f =
enriched_id E₁ x · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f f

enriched_from_arr E₂ f =
enriched_id E₂ (F x) · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) f

f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
enriched_from_arr E₂ f = enriched_from_arr E₂ f

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

 exact (dialgebra_enrichment_id_eq f).
  Defined.

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V

f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_id f
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f f = enriched_id E₁ x

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_id f
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f f = enriched_id E₁ x

    apply EqualizerCommutes.
  Qed.

  Definition dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor
             {x y z : C₁}
             (f₁ : F x --> G x)
             (f₂ : F y --> G y)
             (f₃ : F z --> G z)
    : dialgebra_enrichment_mor f₂ f₃ ⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor f₁ f₂
      -->
      E₁ ⦃ x, z ⦄
    := dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃ #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
       · enriched_comp _ _ _ _.

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor f₁ f₂ f₃
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f₁ f₃ =
dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor f₁ f₂ f₃
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f₁ f₃

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor f₁ f₂ f₃
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f₁ f₃ =
dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor f₁ f₂ f₃
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f₁ f₃

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· enriched_comp E₁ x y z
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f₁ f₃ =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· enriched_comp E₁ x y z
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f₁ f₃

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂

f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· enriched_comp E₁ x y z
· (GE x z · precomp_arr E₂ (G z) f₁) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· enriched_comp E₁ x y z
· (FE x z · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) f₃)

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category

f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (enriched_comp E₁ x y z
   · (GE x z · precomp_arr E₂ (G z) f₁)) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (enriched_comp E₁ x y z
   · (FE x z · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) f₃))

#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (enriched_comp E₁ x y z · GE x z
   · precomp_arr E₂ (G z) f₁) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (enriched_comp E₁ x y z · FE x z
   · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) f₃)

f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (GE y z #⊗ GE x y
   · enriched_comp E₂ (G x) (G y) (G z)
   · precomp_arr E₂ (G z) f₁) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (FE y z #⊗ FE x y
   · enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (F z)
   · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) f₃)

f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧

f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (GE y z #⊗ GE x y
   · (enriched_comp E₂ (G x) (G y) (G z)
      · precomp_arr E₂ (G z) f₁)) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (FE y z #⊗ FE x y
   · (enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (F z)
      · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) f₃))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (GE y z #⊗ GE x y
   · (identity (E₂ ⦃ G y, G z ⦄)
      #⊗ precomp_arr E₂ (G y) f₁
      · enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (G y) (G z))) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (FE y z #⊗ FE x y
   · (enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (F z)
      · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) f₃))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (GE y z #⊗ GE x y
   · (identity (E₂ ⦃ G y, G z ⦄)
      #⊗ precomp_arr E₂ (G y) f₁
      · enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (G y) (G z))) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· (FE y z #⊗ FE x y
   · (postcomp_arr E₂ (F y) f₃
      #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (G z)))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· GE y z #⊗ GE x y
· identity (E₂ ⦃ G y, G z ⦄)
  #⊗ precomp_arr E₂ (G y) f₁
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (G y) (G z) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₂ f₃
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₂
· FE y z #⊗ FE x y
· postcomp_arr E₂ (F y) f₃
  #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (G z)

    exact (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl_eq f₂ f₃).
  Qed.

x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor f₁ f₂ f₃
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left f₁ f₃ =
dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor f₁ f₂ f₃
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right f₁ f₃
 exact (dialgebra_enrichment_comp_eq f₁ f₂ f₃).
  Defined.

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y, z: C₁
f₁: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
f₂: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
f₃: C₂ ⟦ F z, G z ⟧
dialgebra_enrichment_comp f₁ f₂ f₃
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f₁ f₃ =
dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor f₁ f₂ f₃

    apply EqualizerCommutes.
  Qed.

  Definition dialgebra_enrichment_to_arr_mor
             {x y : C₁}
             {f : F x --> G x}
             {g : F y --> G y}
             (h : I_{V} --> dialgebra_enrichment_mor f g)
    :  x --> y
    := enriched_to_arr E₁ (h · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl _ _).

· enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (G y)

      · (mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
         · (enriched_from_arr E₂ g
            #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (G y))))) =
h
· (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g
   · (FE x y · postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) g))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
x, y: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
h: V ⟦ I_{ V}, dialgebra_enrichment_mor f g ⟧
p: dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g · GE x y
· precomp_arr E₂ (G y) f =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g · FE x y
· postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) g
mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
· (enriched_from_arr E₂ g
   #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (G y)) =
postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) g

    
V: monoidal_cat

x, y: C₁
f: C₂ ⟦ F x, G x ⟧
g: C₂ ⟦ F y, G y ⟧
h: V ⟦ I_{ V}, dialgebra_enrichment_mor f g ⟧
p: dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g · GE x y
· precomp_arr E₂ (G y) f =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl f g · FE x y
· postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) g
mon_linvunitor (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
· enriched_from_arr E₂ g #⊗ identity (E₂ ⦃ F x, F y ⦄)
· enriched_comp E₂ (F x) (F y) (G y) =
postcomp_arr E₂ (F x) g

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g)

   #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_comp (pr2 w) (pr2 x)

E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
w, x, y, z: dialgebra F G
dialgebra_enrichment_comp (pr2 x) (pr2 y) (pr2 z)
#⊗ identity (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 w) (pr2 x))
· dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor (pr2 w) (pr2 x)
    (pr2 z) =
mon_lassociator
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 y) (pr2 z))
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 x) (pr2 y))
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 w) (pr2 x))
· (identity (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 y) (pr2 z))
   #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_comp (pr2 w) (pr2 x)
        (pr2 y)
   · dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor (pr2 w) (pr2 y)
       (pr2 z))

· identity (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 y) (pr2 z))
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_comp (pr2 w) (pr2 x) (pr2 y)
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 y) (pr2 z)
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 w) (pr2 y)
· enriched_comp E₁ (pr1 w) (pr1 y) (pr1 z)

    (E₁ ⦃ pr1 x, pr1 y ⦄) (E₁ ⦃ pr1 w, pr1 x ⦄)
· identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 y, pr1 z ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_comp E₁ (pr1 w) (pr1 x) (pr1 y) =
mon_lassociator
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 y) (pr2 z))
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 x) (pr2 y))
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 w) (pr2 x))

  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_comp (pr2 w) (pr2 x) (pr2 y)
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 y) (pr2 z)
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 w) (pr2 y)

FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
f: dialgebra F G
pr1
  (enriched_to_arr dialgebra_enrichment_data
     (enriched_id dialgebra_enrichment_data f)) =
pr1 (identity f)

mon_rinvunitor (dialgebra_enrichment ⦃ g, h ⦄)
· identity (dialgebra_enrichment ⦃ g, h ⦄)
  #⊗ enriched_from_arr dialgebra_enrichment τ
· enriched_comp dialgebra_enrichment f g h

· (mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ pr1 g, pr1 h ⦄)
   · identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 g, pr1 h ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
   · enriched_comp E₁ (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr1 h))

τ: dialgebra F G ⟦ f, g ⟧
mon_rinvunitor
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 g) (pr2 h))
· identity (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 g) (pr2 h))
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_from_arr (pr1 τ) (pr2 τ)
· dialgebra_enrichment_comp (pr2 f) (pr2 g) (pr2 h)
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 h) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 g) (pr2 h)
· (mon_rinvunitor (E₁ ⦃ pr1 g, pr1 h ⦄)
   · identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 g, pr1 h ⦄)
     #⊗ enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
   · enriched_comp E₁ (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr1 h))

GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
f, g, h: dialgebra F G
τ: dialgebra F G ⟦ f, g ⟧
mon_linvunitor
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))
· (dialgebra_enrichment_from_arr (pr1 τ) (pr2 τ)
   · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g))
  #⊗ (identity
        (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))
      · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄)
   · enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
     #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
f, g, h: dialgebra F G
τ: dialgebra F G ⟦ f, g ⟧
mon_linvunitor
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))
· (dialgebra_enrichment_from_arr (pr1 τ) (pr2 τ)
   · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g))
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄)
   · enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
     #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V

f, g, h: dialgebra F G

mon_linvunitor
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))
· enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄)
   · enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
     #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V

GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
f, g, h: dialgebra F G
τ: dialgebra F G ⟦ f, g ⟧
mon_linvunitor
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))
· (identity I_{ V}
   #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)
   · enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
     #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄)) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)
· (mon_linvunitor (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄)
   · enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
     #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄))

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂

E₂: enrichment C₂ V

GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
f, g, h: dialgebra F G
τ: dialgebra F G ⟦ f, g ⟧
mon_linvunitor
  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))
· identity I_{ V}
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)
· enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
  #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)
· mon_linvunitor (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄)
· enriched_from_arr E₁ (pr1 τ)
  #⊗ identity (E₁ ⦃ pr1 h, pr1 f ⦄)

f, g, h: dialgebra F G

  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))

  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f) =

  (dialgebra_enrichment_mor (pr2 h) (pr2 f))
· identity I_{ V}
  #⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 h) (pr2 f)

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  (**
   2. Enrichment of the first projection
   *)

functor_enrichment (dialgebra_pr1 F G)
  dialgebra_enrichment E₁

functor_enrichment (dialgebra_pr1 F G)
  dialgebra_enrichment E₁

functor_enrichment_data (dialgebra_pr1 F G)
  dialgebra_enrichment E₁

(λ FE : functor_enrichment_data (dialgebra_pr1 F G)
          dialgebra_enrichment E₁,
 is_functor_enrichment FE) ?pr1

 exact (λ f g, dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g)).

 is_functor_enrichment FE)
  (λ f g : dialgebra F G,
   dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g))
 
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
∏ x : dialgebra F G,
enriched_id dialgebra_enrichment x
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 x) =
enriched_id E₁ (dialgebra_pr1 F G x)
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V

E₂: enrichment C₂ V

GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
∏ x y z : dialgebra F G,
enriched_comp dialgebra_enrichment x y z
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 z) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 y) (pr2 z)
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 y)
· enriched_comp E₁ (dialgebra_pr1 F G x)
    (dialgebra_pr1 F G y) (dialgebra_pr1 F G z)

GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
∏ (x y : dialgebra F G) (f : dialgebra F G ⟦ x, y ⟧),
enriched_from_arr E₁ (# (dialgebra_pr1 F G) f) =
enriched_from_arr dialgebra_enrichment f
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 y)

      
V: monoidal_cat

enriched_id dialgebra_enrichment x
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 x) =
enriched_id E₁ (dialgebra_pr1 F G x)
 abstract
          (intro f ; cbn ;
           apply dialgebra_enrichment_id_incl).
      
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V

∏ x y z : dialgebra F G,
enriched_comp dialgebra_enrichment x y z
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 z) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 y) (pr2 z)
#⊗ dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 y)
· enriched_comp E₁ (dialgebra_pr1 F G x)
    (dialgebra_pr1 F G y) (dialgebra_pr1 F G z)
 abstract
          (intros x y z ; cbn ;
           apply dialgebra_enrichment_comp_incl).
      
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
∏ (x y : dialgebra F G) (f : dialgebra F G ⟦ x, y ⟧),
enriched_from_arr E₁ (# (dialgebra_pr1 F G) f) =
enriched_from_arr dialgebra_enrichment f
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 x) (pr2 y)
 abstract
          (intros x y f ; cbn ;
           refine (!_) ;
           apply dialgebra_enrichment_from_arr_incl).
  Defined.

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
nat_trans_enrichment (dialgebra_nat_trans F G)
  (functor_comp_enrichment dialgebra_pr1_enrichment FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment dialgebra_pr1_enrichment GE)

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
nat_trans_enrichment (dialgebra_nat_trans F G)
  (functor_comp_enrichment dialgebra_pr1_enrichment FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment dialgebra_pr1_enrichment GE)

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
∏ x y : dialgebra F G,
functor_comp_enrichment dialgebra_pr1_enrichment GE x
  y
· precomp_arr E₂ ((dialgebra_pr1 F G ∙ G) y)
    (dialgebra_nat_trans F G x) =
functor_comp_enrichment dialgebra_pr1_enrichment FE x
  y
· postcomp_arr E₂ ((dialgebra_pr1 F G ∙ F) x)
    (dialgebra_nat_trans F G y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
f, g: dialgebra F G
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g)
· GE (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
· precomp_arr E₂ (G (pr1 g)) (pr2 f) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g)
· FE (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
· postcomp_arr E₂ (F (pr1 f)) (pr2 g)

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
f, g: dialgebra F G
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g)
· (GE (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
   · precomp_arr E₂ (G (pr1 g)) (pr2 f)) =
dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 f) (pr2 g)
· (FE (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
   · postcomp_arr E₂ (F (pr1 f)) (pr2 g))

    exact (dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl_eq (pr2 f) (pr2 g)).
  Qed.

  (**
   3. Enrichment of functors to dialgebras
   *)
  Section FunctorToDialgebraEnrichment.
    Context {C₀ : category}
            {E₀ : enrichment C₀ V}
            {K : C₀ ⟶ C₁}
            {EK : functor_enrichment K E₀ E₁}
            (τ : K ∙ F ⟹ K ∙ G)
            (Eτ : nat_trans_enrichment
                    τ
                    (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
                    (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)).

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
K: C₀ ⟶ C₁
EK: functor_enrichment K E₀ E₁
τ: K ∙ F ⟹ K ∙ G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)
x, y: C₀
EK x y · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left (τ x) (τ y) =
EK x y · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right (τ x) (τ y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V

F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂

E₂: enrichment C₂ V

GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂

E₀: enrichment C₀ V
K: C₀ ⟶ C₁
EK: functor_enrichment K E₀ E₁
τ: K ∙ F ⟹ K ∙ G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)
x, y: C₀
EK x y · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_left (τ x) (τ y) =
EK x y · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right (τ x) (τ y)

      
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V

EK: functor_enrichment K E₀ E₁
τ: K ∙ F ⟹ K ∙ G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)
x, y: C₀
EK x y
· (GE (K x) (K y) · precomp_arr E₂ (G (K y)) (τ x)) =
EK x y
· (FE (K x) (K y) · postcomp_arr E₂ (F (K x)) (τ y))

      
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
K: C₀ ⟶ C₁
EK: functor_enrichment K E₀ E₁
τ: K ∙ F ⟹ K ∙ G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)
x, y: C₀
EK x y · GE (K x) (K y)
· precomp_arr E₂ (G (K y)) (τ x) =
EK x y · FE (K x) (K y)
· postcomp_arr E₂ (F (K x)) (τ y)

      exact (nat_trans_enrichment_to_comp Eτ x y).
    Qed.

EK x y · dialgebra_enrichment_mor_right (τ x) (τ y)
 exact (nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor_eq x y).
    Defined.

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
K: C₀ ⟶ C₁
EK: functor_enrichment K E₀ E₁
τ: K ∙ F ⟹ K ∙ G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)
x, y: C₀
nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor x y
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (τ x) (τ y) = EK x y

      apply EqualizerCommutes.
    Qed.

V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂

  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)
∏ x : C₀,
enriched_id E₀ x
· nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor x x =
enriched_id dialgebra_enrichment
  (nat_trans_to_dialgebra K τ x)
 abstract
            (intros x ;
             use dialgebra_enrichment_mor_eq_of_mor ; cbn ;
             rewrite !assoc' ;
             rewrite nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl ;
             rewrite dialgebra_enrichment_id_incl ;
             apply (functor_enrichment_id EK)).
        
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
K: C₀ ⟶ C₁
EK: functor_enrichment K E₀ E₁
τ: K ∙ F ⟹ K ∙ G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)
∏ x y z : C₀,
enriched_comp E₀ x y z
· nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor x z =
nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor y z
#⊗ nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor x y
· enriched_comp dialgebra_enrichment
    (nat_trans_to_dialgebra K τ x)
    (nat_trans_to_dialgebra K τ y)
    (nat_trans_to_dialgebra K τ z)
 abstract
            (intros x y z ;
             use dialgebra_enrichment_mor_eq_of_mor ; cbn ;
             rewrite !assoc' ;
             rewrite nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl ;
             rewrite dialgebra_enrichment_comp_incl ;
             refine (functor_enrichment_comp EK x y z @ _) ;
             unfold dialgebra_enrichment_comp_mor ;
             rewrite !assoc ;
             apply maponpaths_2 ;
             refine (_ @ tensor_comp_mor _ _ _ _) ;
             rewrite !nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl ;
             apply idpath).

  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)

· nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor x y

            (intros x y f ;
             use dialgebra_enrichment_mor_eq_of_mor ; cbn ;
             rewrite !assoc' ;
             rewrite nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl ;
             rewrite dialgebra_enrichment_from_arr_incl ;
             apply (functor_enrichment_from_arr EK)).
    Defined.

EK x y
· precomp_arr E₁ (K y)
    (nat_trans_to_dialgebra_pr1 K τ x) =

  nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment
  dialgebra_pr1_enrichment x y
· postcomp_arr E₁
    ((nat_trans_to_dialgebra K τ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G)
       x) (nat_trans_to_dialgebra_pr1 K τ y)

  (functor_comp_enrichment EK FE)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EK GE)

EK x y · precomp_arr E₁ (K y) (identity (K x)) =
nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor x y
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (τ x) (τ y)
· postcomp_arr E₁ (K x) (identity (K y))

      apply nat_trans_to_dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl.
    Qed.
  End FunctorToDialgebraEnrichment.

  (**
   4. Enrichment of natural transformations to dialgebras
   *)
  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
H₁, H₂: C₀ ⟶ dialgebra F G
EH₁: functor_enrichment H₁ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
EH₂: functor_enrichment H₂ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
τ: H₁ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G ⟹ H₂ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₁
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₂
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
p: ∏ x : C₀,
pr2 (H₁ x) · # G (τ x) = # F (τ x) · pr2 (H₂ x)
nat_trans_enrichment
  (build_nat_trans_to_dialgebra H₁ H₂ τ p) EH₁ EH₂

  
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
H₁, H₂: C₀ ⟶ dialgebra F G
EH₁: functor_enrichment H₁ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
EH₂: functor_enrichment H₂ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
τ: H₁ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G ⟹ H₂ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₁
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₂
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
p: ∏ x : C₀,
pr2 (H₁ x) · # G (τ x) = # F (τ x) · pr2 (H₂ x)
nat_trans_enrichment
  (build_nat_trans_to_dialgebra H₁ H₂ τ p) EH₁ EH₂

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
H₁, H₂: C₀ ⟶ dialgebra F G
EH₁: functor_enrichment H₁ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
EH₂: functor_enrichment H₂ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
τ: H₁ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G ⟹ H₂ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₁
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₂
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
p: ∏ x : C₀,
pr2 (H₁ x) · # G (τ x) = # F (τ x) · pr2 (H₂ x)
∏ x y : C₀,
EH₂ x y
· precomp_arr dialgebra_enrichment (H₂ y)
    (build_nat_trans_to_dialgebra H₁ H₂ τ p x) =
EH₁ x y
· postcomp_arr dialgebra_enrichment (H₁ x)
    (build_nat_trans_to_dialgebra H₁ H₂ τ p y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
H₁, H₂: C₀ ⟶ dialgebra F G
EH₁: functor_enrichment H₁ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
EH₂: functor_enrichment H₂ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
τ: H₁ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G ⟹ H₂ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₁
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₂
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
p: ∏ x : C₀,
pr2 (H₁ x) · # G (τ x) = # F (τ x) · pr2 (H₂ x)
x, y: C₀
EH₂ x y
· precomp_arr dialgebra_enrichment (H₂ y) (τ x,, p x) =
EH₁ x y
· postcomp_arr dialgebra_enrichment (H₁ x) (τ y,, p y)

    
V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
H₁, H₂: C₀ ⟶ dialgebra F G
EH₁: functor_enrichment H₁ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
EH₂: functor_enrichment H₂ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
τ: H₁ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G ⟹ H₂ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₁
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₂
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
p: ∏ x : C₀,
pr2 (H₁ x) · # G (τ x) = # F (τ x) · pr2 (H₂ x)
x, y: C₀
EH₂ x y
· precomp_arr dialgebra_enrichment (H₂ y) (τ x,, p x)
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 (H₁ x))
    (pr2 (H₂ y)) =
EH₁ x y
· postcomp_arr dialgebra_enrichment (H₁ x) (τ y,, p y)
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 (H₁ x))
    (pr2 (H₂ y))

EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
H₁, H₂: C₀ ⟶ dialgebra F G
EH₁: functor_enrichment H₁ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
EH₂: functor_enrichment H₂ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
τ: H₁ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G ⟹ H₂ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₁
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₂
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)

       (pr2 (H₂ y)))

V: monoidal_cat
EV: Equalizers V
C₁, C₂: category
F, G: C₁ ⟶ C₂
E₁: enrichment C₁ V
E₂: enrichment C₂ V
FE: functor_enrichment F E₁ E₂
GE: functor_enrichment G E₁ E₂
C₀: category
E₀: enrichment C₀ V
H₁, H₂: C₀ ⟶ dialgebra F G
EH₁: functor_enrichment H₁ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
EH₂: functor_enrichment H₂ E₀ dialgebra_enrichment
τ: H₁ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G ⟹ H₂ ∙ dialgebra_pr1 F G
Eτ: nat_trans_enrichment τ
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₁
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
  (functor_comp_enrichment EH₂
     dialgebra_pr1_enrichment)
p: ∏ x : C₀,
pr2 (H₁ x) · # G (τ x) = # F (τ x) · pr2 (H₂ x)
x, y: C₀
EH₂ x y
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 (H₂ x))
    (pr2 (H₂ y))
· precomp_arr E₁ (pr1 (H₂ y)) (pr1 (τ x,, p x)) =
EH₁ x y
· dialgebra_enrichment_mor_incl (pr2 (H₁ x))
    (pr2 (H₁ y))
· postcomp_arr E₁ (pr1 (H₁ x)) (pr1 (τ y,, p y))

    exact (nat_trans_enrichment_to_comp Eτ x y).
  Qed.
End EnrichedDialgebras.
